<div class="reflist" style="list-style-type: lower-alpha;">
<div class="mw-references-wrap"><ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-1"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-1">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Certain award groups do not simply award one winner. They recognize several different recipients, have runners-up and have third place. Since this is a specific recognition and is different from losing an award, runner-up mentions are considered wins in this award tally. Awards in certain categories do not have prior nominations and only winners are announced by the jury. For simplification and to avoid errors, each award in this list has been presumed to have had a prior nomination.</span>
</li>
</ol></div></div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><a href="/wiki/Americans" title="Americans">American</a> singer and songwriter <a href="/wiki/Carrie_Underwood" title="Carrie Underwood">Carrie Underwood</a> has received many awards and nominations for her work across music, film, television and fashion. She has released thus far six studio albums and one greatest hits collection — <i><a href="/wiki/Some_Hearts_(Carrie_Underwood_album)" class="mw-redirect" title="Some Hearts (Carrie Underwood album)">Some Hearts</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Carnival_Ride" title="Carnival Ride">Carnival Ride</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Play_On_(Carrie_Underwood_album)" title="Play On (Carrie Underwood album)">Play On</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Blown_Away_(album)" title="Blown Away (album)">Blown Away</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Greatest_Hits:_Decade_Number_1" title="Greatest Hits: Decade Number 1">Greatest Hits: Decade Number 1</a></i>,  <i><a href="/wiki/Storyteller_(Carrie_Underwood_album)" title="Storyteller (Carrie Underwood album)">Storyteller</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Cry_Pretty" title="Cry Pretty">Cry Pretty</a></i>.
</p><p>Among 170 worldwide awards, Underwood has won seven <a href="/wiki/Grammy_Awards" class="mw-redirect" title="Grammy Awards">Grammy Awards</a> and became, in 2007, only the second country artist in history to win the <a href="/wiki/Grammy_Award_for_Best_New_Artist" title="Grammy Award for Best New Artist">Grammy Award for Best New Artist</a>.  She is also the first <i><a href="/wiki/American_Idol" title="American Idol">American Idol</a></i> winner to sweep all three major music awards in one season (<a href="/wiki/American_Music_Award" class="mw-redirect" title="American Music Award">American Music</a>, <a href="/wiki/Billboard_Music_Awards" class="mw-redirect" title="Billboard Music Awards">Billboard Music</a>, and Grammy Awards).
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Academy_of_Country_Music_Awards">Academy of Country Music Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Academy of Country Music Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Academy_of_Country_Music_Awards" title="Academy of Country Music Awards">Academy of Country Music Awards</a> is an annual country music awards show, the first ever created, established in 1964. In 2010, Underwood made history by becoming the first woman to ever receive the <a href="/wiki/Academy_of_Country_Music_Award_for_Entertainer_of_the_Year" title="Academy of Country Music Award for Entertainer of the Year">Entertainer of the Year Award</a> twice, in addition to being the first to ever win the award consecutively.<sup id="cite_ref-Abclocal.go.com_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Abclocal.go.com-2">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> In 2014, she won the Gene Weed Special Achievement Award, for her widespread exposure through <a href="/wiki/National_Football_League" title="National Football League">National Football League</a> <a href="/wiki/NBC_Sunday_Night_Football" title="NBC Sunday Night Football">NBC Sunday Night Football</a>, the NBC broadcast of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Sound_of_Music_Live!" title="The Sound of Music Live!">The Sound of Music Live!</a></i>, her <i><a href="/wiki/Blown_Away_Tour" title="Blown Away Tour">Blown Away Tour</a></i> and her charity work with the <a href="/wiki/American_Red_Cross" title="American Red Cross">American Red Cross</a> and her C.A.T.S. Foundation.<sup id="cite_ref-auto_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-3">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> She is also the first person to win the ACM Lifting Lives Gary Haber Award, which recognizes a country music artist or industry professional "who is committed to serving others, has a generosity of spirit and shows a dedication to helping those in need".<sup id="cite_ref-acmcountry.com_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-acmcountry.com-4">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Underwood is one of the most awarded women in the history of the ACM Awards.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> She has won a total of 14 ACM Awards.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="American_Country_Awards">American Country Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: American Country Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/American_Country_Awards" title="American Country Awards">American Country Awards</a> was a country music awards show, entirely voted on by fans. Created by the Fox Network, the awards honored country music artists in music, video, and touring categories. It lasted four years. Underwood won twelve awards, more than any other artist.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="American_Country_Countdown_Awards">American Country Countdown Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: American Country Countdown Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/American_Country_Countdown_Awards" title="American Country Countdown Awards">American Country Countdown Awards</a> is an annual country music awards show that honors artists based on their album sales, touring data and the amount of their radio airplay.<sup id="cite_ref-rolling_stone_performers_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-rolling_stone_performers-22">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> It is named after the long-running radio show <a href="/wiki/American_Country_Countdown" title="American Country Countdown">American Country Countdown</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-rolling_stone_announcement_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-rolling_stone_announcement-23">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="American_Music_Awards">American Music Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: American Music Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/American_Music_Awards" title="American Music Awards">American Music Awards</a> is an annual major American music award show by the American Broadcasting Company, presented since 1973. Underwood has won thirteen awards out of eighteen nominations. She is the only artist in AMA history to have won Favorite Country Album for every studio album released.<sup id="cite_ref-AMA_2016_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AMA_2016-26">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Billboard_Music_Awards">Billboard Music Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Billboard Music Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Billboard_Music_Award" title="Billboard Music Award">Billboard Music Award</a> is an honor given by <i><a href="/wiki/Billboard_(magazine)" title="Billboard (magazine)">Billboard</a></i>, the preeminent publication covering the music business. Finalists are based on United States year-end chart performance according to Nielsen data for sales, number of downloads and total airplay.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="BMI_Awards">BMI Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: BMI Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Broadcast_Music,_Incorporated" class="mw-redirect" title="Broadcast Music, Incorporated">Broadcast Music, Incorporated</a> (BMI) Awards is an annual award show hosted for the purpose of giving awards to songwriters. Songwriters are selected each year from the entire BMI catalog, based on the number of performances during the award period. Underwood has been honored with 14 BMI Country awards for songwriting.<sup id="cite_ref-2017_Honors_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2017_Honors-45">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> She has also won 14 BMI Million-Air Awards, which are acknowledgements of songs that have achieved one million or more spins on radio.<sup id="cite_ref-2017_Honors_45-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2017_Honors-45">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> Additionally, at the 69th annual BMI/NAB Dinner in 2017, Underwood received the BMI Board of Directors Award, for the impact her music has had on the broadcast industry, as well as her many contributions as a songwriter.<sup id="cite_ref-2017_Honors_45-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2017_Honors-45">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="British_Country_Music_Awards">British Country Music Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: British Country Music Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The British Country Music Awards (BCM Awards) are held annually by the British Country Music Association to honor national and international success for Country music artists familiar to the United Kingdom. Underwood has won once.

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Celebrity_Fight_Night">Celebrity Fight Night</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Celebrity Fight Night">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Celebrity Fight Night Foundation, Inc. is a non-profit organization that was established to promote ongoing efforts to eliminate sickness and poverty. It annually holds the <a href="/wiki/Muhammad_Ali" title="Muhammad Ali">Muhammad Ali</a>'s "Celebrity Fight Night" charity event.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> The Foundation also established the "Muhammad Ali Celebrity Fight Night Award", which acknowledges leaders in the sports, entertainment and business communities who best represent the qualities associated with the Alis' fight to find a cure for Parkinson's disease.<sup id="cite_ref-Celebrity_Fight_Night_57-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Celebrity_Fight_Night-57">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> Underwood received the award in 2016.
</p>

<th scope="col" style="width:6%;"><abbr title="Reference(s)">Ref.</abbr>

<td>Muhammad Ali Celebrity Fight Night Award</td>
<td style="background: #99FF99; color: black; vertical-align: middle; text-align: center;" class="yes table-yes2">Won</td>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Clio_Awards">Clio Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Clio Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Clio_Awards" title="Clio Awards">Clio Awards</a> is an annual award program that recognizes innovation and creative excellence in advertising, design and communication, as judged by an international panel of advertising professionals. It has been held since 1960.

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Country_Music_Association_Awards">Country Music Association Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Country Music Association Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Country_Music_Association_Awards" title="Country Music Association Awards">Country Music Association Awards</a> is an annual country music awards show, established in 1967. Underwood has won eighth awards, including both the Chairman's Award and International Artist Achievement award, which recognizes outstanding achievement by a U.S.-based artist who contributes to the awareness and development of country music worldwide.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-CMA_2017_60-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CMA_2017-60">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Country_Music_Awards_of_Australia">Country Music Awards of Australia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Country Music Awards of Australia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Country_Music_Awards_of_Australia" title="Country Music Awards of Australia">Country Music Awards of Australia</a> are held by the <a href="/wiki/Country_Music_Association_of_Australia" title="Country Music Association of Australia">Country Music Association of Australia</a> to celebrate recording excellence in the Australian country music industry. They were originally established in 1973.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> Underwood has won once.
</p>
<table class="wikitable plainrowheaders" style="width:85%;">

<tbody><tr>
<th scope="col" style="width:4%;">Year
</th>
<th scope="col" style="width:35%;">Nominated work / Recipient
</th>
<th scope="col" style="width:50%;">Category
</th>
<th scope="col" style="width:6%;">Result
</th>
<th scope="col" style="width:6%;"><abbr title="Reference(s)">Ref.</abbr>
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td>2013
</td>
<td><a href="/wiki/Blown_Away_(album)" title="Blown Away (album)">Blown Away</a>
</td>
<td>Top Selling International Album of the Year
</td>
<td style="background: #99FF99; color: black; vertical-align: middle; text-align: center;" class="yes table-yes2">Won
</td>
<td><sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
</tbody></table>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="CMT_Awards">CMT Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: CMT Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="CMT_Artists_of_the_Year_Awards">CMT Artists of the Year Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: CMT Artists of the Year Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The CMT Artists of the Year Awards are given by <a href="/wiki/Country_Music_Television" class="mw-redirect" title="Country Music Television">Country Music Television</a> to honor the top country acts of each year. The show was established in 2010. Underwood has been awarded five times.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="CMT_Music_Awards">CMT Music Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: CMT Music Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/CMT_Music_Awards" title="CMT Music Awards">CMT Music Awards</a> is an annual ceremony dedicated exclusively to honor country music videos. It was established in 1967, and had several names throughout the years. In 2002, it was moved to <a href="/wiki/Country_Music_Television" class="mw-redirect" title="Country Music Television">Country Music Television</a> and, in 2005, was renamed CMT Music Awards.
With 20 wins, Underwood is the most awarded artist overall in the show's history.<sup id="cite_ref-CMT_2017_76-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CMT_2017-76">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> She also has the most Video of the Year wins and Female Video of the Year wins.<sup id="cite_ref-CMT_2017_76-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CMT_2017-76">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="CMT_Online_Awards">CMT Online Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: CMT Online Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>CMT Online Awards were an annual online award show, established in 2006 by <a href="/wiki/Country_Music_Television" class="mw-redirect" title="Country Music Television">Country Music Television</a>. This was a "fan-voted" award show, based on the fans going to CMT.com streaming the videos and viewing the artists' pages. The winner in each category received the highest numbers of streams and views on CMT.com.<sup id="cite_ref-CMT_Online_90-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CMT_Online-90">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<table class="wikitable plainrowheaders" style="width:85%;">

<th scope="col" style="width:50%;">Category
</th>
<th scope="col" style="width:6%;">Result
</th>
<th scope="col" style="width:6%;"><abbr title="Reference(s)">Ref.</abbr>
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td rowspan="2">2008</td>
<td>Carrie Underwood</td>
<td>Most Digitally-Active Female Artist</td>
<td style="background: #99FF99; color: black; vertical-align: middle; text-align: center;" class="yes table-yes2">Won</td>
<td rowspan="2"><sup id="cite_ref-CMT_Online_90-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CMT_Online-90">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="CMT_Teddy_Awards">CMT Teddy Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: CMT Teddy Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The CMT Teddy Awards were a special music video award show dedicated to celebrate <a href="/wiki/Valentine%27s_Day" title="Valentine&#39;s Day">Valentine's Day</a>. There were eight categories.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup> Underwood won two awards.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Country_Radio_Seminar">Country Radio Seminar</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Country Radio Seminar">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The Country Radio Seminar (CRS) is one of the largest media gatherings of any kind or of any format in the US founded in 1970 and is held annually by the <a href="/wiki/Country_Radio_Broadcasters" title="Country Radio Broadcasters">Country Radio Broadcasters</a>. The Seminar also honors individuals related to country music with different awards. In 2014, the CRS' Board of Directors awarded Underwood the Artist Humanitarian Award, which was created in 1990 to honor those Country music artists who have exhibited exceptional humanitarian efforts during their career.
</p>
<table class="wikitable plainrowheaders" style="width:85%;">

<tbody><tr>
<th scope="col" style="width:4%;">Year
</th>
<th scope="col" style="width:35%;">Nominated work / Recipient
</th>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="European_Country_Music_Association_Awards">European Country Music Association Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: European Country Music Association Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/European_Country_Music_Association" title="European Country Music Association">European Country Music Association</a> (ECMA) was established in 1994 in the United Kingdom and Spain, Europe, by people related to the European Country music scene, such as publishers, DJs and musics. It originally consisted of less than 100 members and the very first president was UK's Harry E. Fenton. Votes for nominations and winners come only from members of the organization. Underwood won once.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Golden_Globe_Awards">Golden Globe Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Golden Globe Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Golden_Globe_Awards" title="Golden Globe Awards">Golden Globe Awards</a> were established in 1944 by the <a href="/wiki/Hollywood_Foreign_Press_Association" title="Hollywood Foreign Press Association">Hollywood Foreign Press Association</a> to celebrate the best in film and television.

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="GMA_Dove_Awards">GMA Dove Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: GMA Dove Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>A <a href="/wiki/Dove_Award" class="mw-redirect" title="Dove Award">Dove Award</a> is an accolade by the <a href="/wiki/Gospel_Music_Association" title="Gospel Music Association">Gospel Music Association</a> (GMA) of the United States to recognize outstanding achievement in the <a href="/wiki/Christian_music_industry" title="Christian music industry">Christian music industry</a>. The awards are presented, since 1969, at an annual ceremony called the GMA Dove Awards. Underwood won once.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Grammy_Awards">Grammy Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Grammy Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Grammy_Awards" class="mw-redirect" title="Grammy Awards">Grammy Awards</a> are presented annually by the <a href="/wiki/National_Academy_of_Recording_Arts_and_Sciences" class="mw-redirect" title="National Academy of Recording Arts and Sciences">National Academy of Recording Arts and Sciences</a> for outstanding achievements in the music industry. It is presented since 1958. Underwood has won seven awards out of fourteen nominations. In 2007, she became only the second country artist in history to win the <a href="/wiki/Grammy_Award_for_Best_New_Artist" title="Grammy Award for Best New Artist">Best New Artist</a> award, following <a href="/wiki/LeAnn_Rimes" title="LeAnn Rimes">LeAnn Rimes</a> (1997).<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Honors_Gala">Honors Gala</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Honors Gala">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The Honors Gala is an event organized since 1975 by the <a href="/wiki/T.J._Martell_Foundation" class="mw-redirect" title="T.J. Martell Foundation">T.J. Martell Foundation</a>, the music industry's largest foundation that funds innovative medical research focused on finding cures for leukemia, cancer and AIDS. It honors individuals of several areas with different awards. At the 38th event, in 2013, Underwood received the Artist Achievement Award.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="iHeartRadio_Music_Awards">iHeartRadio Music Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: iHeartRadio Music Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Inspirational_Country_Music_Awards">Inspirational Country Music Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Inspirational Country Music Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The Inspirational Country Music Awards are a member-voted award show dedicated to honoring and showcasing the biggest names and emerging talent among artists who perform Christian and inspirational country music.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2017)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Music_Row_Awards">Music Row Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Music Row Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/MusicRow" title="MusicRow">MusicRow</a> Awards is an annual awards show held by Nashville's music industry publication, MusicRow. The winners are selected by over 300 managers, musicians, songwriters, publishers and label executives. Underwood was awarded once.

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Nashville_Songwriters_Association_International_Awards">Nashville Songwriters Association International Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Nashville Songwriters Association International Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Nashville_Songwriters_Association_International" title="Nashville Songwriters Association International">Nashville Songwriters Association International</a> (NSAI) hosts industry professionals each year for the "World's Largest #1 Party", in association with the <a href="/wiki/Recording_Academy" class="mw-redirect" title="Recording Academy">Recording Academy</a>, to celebrate veteran hitmakers and talented new artists.
</p>

<h2><span id="Nashville_Symphony.27s_Harmony"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Nashville_Symphony's_Harmony">Nashville Symphony's Harmony</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Nashville Symphony&#039;s Harmony">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The Nashville Symphony's Harmony award is presented to individuals who have demonstrated continued interest and support of music in Nashville, exemplify the connections between the diverse music of the city and have contributed to the development and appreciation of music culture. It is presented during the annual Symphony Ball on Saturday at the Schermerhorn Symphony Center in downtown Nashville.<sup id="cite_ref-NSH_121-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NSH-121">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span id="People.27s_Choice_Awards"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="People's_Choice_Awards">People's Choice Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: People&#039;s Choice Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/People%27s_Choice_Awards" title="People&#39;s Choice Awards">People's Choice Awards</a> is an American awards show recognizing the people and the work of <a href="/wiki/Popular_culture" title="Popular culture">popular culture</a>. The show has been held annually since 1975 and is a venue for the general public to honor their favorite actors and actresses, musical performers, television shows and motion pictures. Underwood has won nine awards, out of eighteen nominations.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Pollstar_Awards">Pollstar Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Pollstar Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <i><a href="/wiki/Pollstar" title="Pollstar">Pollstar</a></i> Awards is ceremony to honor artists and professionals in the concert industry. It was created by <i>Pollstar</i>, the leading trade publication for the concert tour industry.

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Teen_Choice_Awards">Teen Choice Awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Teen Choice Awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Teen_Choice_Awards" title="Teen Choice Awards">Teen Choice Awards</a> is an annual show that honors the years biggest achievements in music, movies, sports, television, fashion and more. Underwood has won seven awards out of nineteen nominations.

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_honors">Other honors</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Other honors">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Grand_Ole_Opry">Grand Ole Opry</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Grand Ole Opry">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Grand_Ole_Opry" title="Grand Ole Opry">Grand Ole Opry</a> has been called the "Home of American Music" and "Country's most famous stage".<sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup> Membership in the Opry remains one of Country Music's crowning achievements.<sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup> Being made a member of the Grand Ole Opry, Country Music's big house, the oldest, most enduring "Hall of Fame," is to be identified as a member of the elite of Country Music.
</p>

</th></tr>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Guinness_World_Records">Guinness World Records</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Guinness World Records">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <i><a href="/wiki/Guinness_World_Records" title="Guinness World Records">Guinness World Records</a></i> honors the year's most impressive acts. Underwood has set one record.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hollywood_Walk_of_Fame">Hollywood Walk of Fame</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Hollywood Walk of Fame">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Hollywood_Walk_of_Fame" title="Hollywood Walk of Fame">Hollywood Walk of Fame</a> is a <a href="/wiki/Sidewalk" title="Sidewalk">sidewalk</a> along <a href="/wiki/Hollywood_Boulevard" title="Hollywood Boulevard">Hollywood Boulevard</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vine_Street" title="Vine Street">Vine Street</a> in <a href="/wiki/Hollywood,_California" class="mw-redirect" title="Hollywood, California">Hollywood, California</a>, United States, that serves as an entertainment <a href="/wiki/Hall_of_fame" class="mw-redirect" title="Hall of fame">hall of fame</a>. It is embedded with more than 2,000 five-pointed stars featuring the names of <a href="/wiki/Celebrity" title="Celebrity">celebrities</a> honored by the Hollywood <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_commerce" title="Chamber of commerce">Chamber of Commerce</a> for their contributions to the entertainment industry. Underwood is part of the Class of 2018 of inductees.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Oklahoma_Hall_of_Fame">Oklahoma Hall of Fame</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Oklahoma Hall of Fame">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The Oklahoma Memorial Association was founded in 1927 with the purpose of establishing the <a href="/wiki/Oklahoma_Hall_of_Fame" title="Oklahoma Hall of Fame">Oklahoma Hall of Fame</a>. Being inducted into the Oklahoma Hall of Fame is considered to be the highest honor one can receive from the state.<sup id="cite_ref-OHA_156-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OHA-156">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup> Underwood was inducted in 2017.
</p>

</th>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Oklahoma_Music_Hall_of_Fame">Oklahoma Music Hall of Fame</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Oklahoma Music Hall of Fame">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Oklahoma_Music_Hall_of_Fame" title="Oklahoma Music Hall of Fame">Oklahoma Music Hall of Fame</a> honors Oklahoma musicians for their lifetime achievements in music. The induction ceremony and concert is held each year in Muskogee. Underwood was inducted in 2009. She had previously been named the Hall's Rising Star in 2005.
</p>
